1)SELECT count( * )
  FROM lineitem
 WHERE ( l_receiptdate BETWEEN '1993-03-01' AND '1993-03-31' ) 
       OR
        ( l_receiptdate BETWEEN '1993-06-01' AND '1993-06-31' );


#|count ( * )
-+-----------
1|1411       

    
2)SELECT count( * )
  FROM customer, 
       orders, 
       lineitem
 WHERE c_custkey = o_custkey 
       AND
       o_orderkey = l_orderkey 
       AND
        ( o_orderdate BETWEEN '1993-03-01' AND '1993-03-31' ) 
       AND
       l_quantity >= 2;

#|count ( * )
-+-----------
1|670        

3)SELECT DISTINCT s.ps_partkey
  FROM partsupp s
 WHERE EXISTS ( 
           SELECT s1.ps_partkey
             FROM partsupp s1
            WHERE s.ps_partkey = s1.ps_partkey 
                  AND
                  s.ps_suppkey > s1.ps_suppkey 
       );

4) SELECT DISTINCT p.ps_suppkey
           FROM partsupp p
          WHERE EXISTS ( 
                    SELECT p1.ps_suppkey
                      FROM partsupp p1
                     WHERE p.ps_suppkey = p1.ps_suppkey 
                           AND
                           p.ps_partkey > p1.ps_partkey 
                );

5)SELECT s_name
  FROM supplier, 
       lineitem, 
       part
 WHERE s_suppkey = l_suppkey 
       AND
       l_partkey = p_partkey 
       AND
       p_retailprice IN ( 
           SELECT max( p_retailprice )
             FROM part 
       );

6)SELECT s_name,
       c_name
  FROM supplier s, 
       customer c, 
       orders o, 
       lineitem l
 WHERE c.c_custkey = o.o_custkey 
       AND
       l.l_orderkey = o.o_orderkey 
       AND
       l.l_suppkey = s.s_suppkey 
       AND
       o.o_totalprice >= ( 
           SELECT max( o1.o_totalprice )
             FROM orders o1, 
                  customer c1, 
                  supplier s1, 
                  lineitem l1
            WHERE c1.c_custkey = o1.o_custkey 
                  AND
                  l1.l_orderkey = o1.o_orderkey 
                  AND
                  l1.l_suppkey = s1.s_suppkey 
       );

#|s_name            |c_name            
-+------------------+------------------
1|Supplier#000000001|Customer#000000676
2|Supplier#000000003|Customer#000000676
3|Supplier#000000021|Customer#000000676
4|Supplier#000000029|Customer#000000676
5|Supplier#000000042|Customer#000000676
6|Supplier#000000054|Customer#000000676
7|Supplier#000000080|Customer#000000676


7)SELECT count( * ) AS scount
  FROM supplier, 
       customer, 
       orders,
       lineitem, 
       nation, 
       region
 WHERE c_nationkey = n_nationkey 
       AND
       n_regionkey = r_regionkey 
       AND
       o_custkey = c_custkey 
       and
       o_orderkey = l_orderkey
       and
       s_suppkey = l_suppkey
       AND
       r_name NOT LIKE '%EUROPE%';

#|scount
-+------
1|49334 


 

8)SELECT c_name
  FROM supplier, 
       customer, 
       nation,
       orders,
       lineitem, 
       region
 WHERE c_custkey = o_custkey
       and
       l_orderkey = o_orderkey
       and
       l_suppkey = s_suppkey
       AND
       s_nationkey = n_nationkey
       and
       n_regionkey = r_regionkey 
       AND
       r_name LIKE '%ASIA%';

9)SELECT DISTINCT p.p_name,
                p.p_retailprice
           FROM part p, 
                partsupp ps, 
                supplier s, 
                nation n, 
                region r
          WHERE p.p_partkey = ps.ps_partkey 
                AND
                ps.ps_suppkey = s.s_suppkey 
                AND
                s.s_nationkey = n.n_nationkey 
                AND
                n.n_regionkey = r.r_regionkey 
                AND
                 ( r.r_name LIKE '%EUROPE%' ) 
                AND
                p.p_retailprice IN ( 
                    SELECT min( p1.p_retailprice )
                      FROM part p1, 
                           partsupp ps1, 
                           supplier s1, 
                           nation n1, 
                           region r1
                     WHERE p1.p_partkey = ps1.ps_partkey 
                           AND
                           ps1.ps_suppkey = s1.s_suppkey 
                           AND
                           s1.s_nationkey = n1.n_nationkey 
                           AND
                           n1.n_regionkey = r1.r_regionkey 
                           AND
                           r1.r_name LIKE '%EUROPE%' 
                );

#|p_name                                  |p_retailprice
-+----------------------------------------+-------------
1|goldenrod lavender spring chocolate lace|901          


10)SELECT r_name,
       o_totalprice
  FROM region r, 
       customer c, 
       orders o, 
       nation n
 WHERE r.r_regionkey = n.n_regionkey 
       AND
       c.c_custkey = o.o_orderkey 
       AND
       c.c_nationkey = n.n_nationkey 
       AND
       o.o_totalprice IN ( 
           SELECT max( o1.o_totalprice )
             FROM region r1, 
                  customer c1, 
                  orders o1, 
                  nation n1
            WHERE r1.r_regionkey = n1.n_regionkey 
                  AND
                  c1.c_custkey = o1.o_orderkey 
                  AND
                  c1.c_nationkey = n1.n_nationkey 
       );

#|r_name     |o_totalprice
-+-----------+------------
1|MIDDLE EAST|368220.47
